   193	export function findCompactConfig(
   194	    compactOrAlias: CompactOrAlias,
   195	): CompactConfig | undefined {
   196	    return Object.values(CompactConfigMap).find(
   197	        ({ compact, alias }) =>
   198	            compact === compactOrAlias ||
   199	            alias.includes(compactOrAlias as AnyType),
   200	    );
   201	}

   334	// This type check is a little fragile because it's based on

   336	export const isTableCalculation = (
   337	    item: ItemsMap[string] | AdditionalMetric | Pick<Field, 'table' | 'name'>,
   338	): item is TableCalculation =>
   339	    item
   340	        ? !isCustomDimension(item) &&
   341	          !!('sql' in item && item.sql) &&
   342	          !('description' in item) &&
   343	          !('tableName' in item) &&
   344	          'displayName' in item
   345	        : false;

   362	    label: string; // Friendly name
   363	    table: string; // Table names are unique within the project
   364	    tableLabel: string; // Table friendly name
   365	    sql: string; // Templated sql
   366	    description?: string;
   367	    source?: Source | undefined;
   368	    hidden: boolean;

   374	    /**

   385	export const isField = (field: AnyType): field is Field =>
   386	    field ? !!field.fieldType : false;
   387	
   388	// Field ids are unique across the project
   389	export type FieldId = string;
   390	
   391	export const convertFieldRefToFieldId = (
   392	    fieldRef: string,
   393	    fallbackTableName?: string,
   394	) => {
   395	    const parts = fieldRef.split('.');
   396	    if (parts.length !== 2) {
   397	        if (fallbackTableName) {
   398	            return `${fallbackTableName}_${fieldRef}`;
   399	        }
   400	        throw new CompileError(
   401	            `Table calculation contains an invalid reference: ${fieldRef}. References must be of the format "table.field"`,
   402	            {},
   403	        );
   404	    }
   405	    const [tableName, fieldName] = parts;
   406	
   407	    return `${tableName}_${fieldName}`;
   408	};
   409	
   410	export type Source = {
   411	    path: string;
   412	    range: {
   413	        start: SourcePosition;
   414	        end: SourcePosition;
   415	    };
   416	    highlight?: {
   417	        start: SourcePosition;
   418	        end: SourcePosition;
   419	    };
   420	    content: string;
   421	};
   422	type SourcePosition = {
   423	    line: number;
   424	    character: number;
   425	};
   426	
   427	export enum DimensionType {
   428	    STRING = 'string',
   429	    NUMBER = 'number',
   430	    TIMESTAMP = 'timestamp',
   431	    DATE = 'date',
   432	    BOOLEAN = 'boolean',
   433	}
   434	
   435	export interface Dimension extends Field {
   436	    fieldType: FieldType.DIMENSION;
   437	    type: DimensionType;
   438	    /**
   439	     * @deprecated Use groups property instead.
   440	     */
   441	    group?: string;
   442	    requiredAttributes?: Record<string, string | string[]>;
   443	    timeInterval?: TimeFrames;
   444	    timeIntervalBaseDimensionName?: string;
   445	    isAdditionalDimension?: boolean;
   446	    colors?: Record<string, string>;
   447	    isIntervalBase?: boolean;
   448	    aiHint?: string | string[];
   449	}
   450	
   451	type CompiledProperties = {
   452	    compiledSql: string; // sql string with resolved template variables
   453	    tablesReferences: Array<string> | undefined;
   454	    tablesRequiredAttributes?: Record<
   455	        string,
   456	        Record<string, string | string[]>
   457	    >;
   458	};
   459	export type CompiledDimension = Dimension & CompiledProperties;
   460	export type CompiledMetric = Metric & CompiledProperties;
   461	
   462	export type CompiledField = CompiledDimension | CompiledMetric;
   463	
   464	export const isDimension = (
   465	    field: ItemsMap[string] | AdditionalMetric | undefined, // NOTE: `ItemsMap converts AdditionalMetric to Metric
   466	): field is Dimension =>
   467	    isField(field) && field.fieldType === FieldType.DIMENSION;
   468	
   469	export interface FilterableDimension extends Dimension {
   470	    type:
   471	        | DimensionType.STRING
   472	        | DimensionType.NUMBER
   473	        | DimensionType.DATE
   474	        | DimensionType.TIMESTAMP
   475	        | DimensionType.BOOLEAN;
   476	}
   477	
   478	export type FieldRef = string;
   479	export const getFieldRef = (field: Pick<Field, 'table' | 'name'>): FieldRef =>
   480	    `${field.table}.${field.name}`;
   481	
   482	export const getFieldLabel = (field: Field): string =>
   483	    `${field.tableLabel} ${field.label}`;
   484	
   485	export enum MetricType {
   486	    PERCENTILE = 'percentile',
   487	    AVERAGE = 'average',
   488	    COUNT = 'count',
   489	    COUNT_DISTINCT = 'count_distinct',
   490	    SUM = 'sum',
   491	    MIN = 'min',
   492	    MAX = 'max',
   493	    NUMBER = 'number',
   494	    MEDIAN = 'median',
   495	    STRING = 'string',
   496	    DATE = 'date',
   497	    TIMESTAMP = 'timestamp',
   498	    BOOLEAN = 'boolean',
   499	}
   500	
   501	export enum Format {
   502	    KM = 'km',
   503	    MI = 'mi',
   504	    USD = 'usd',
   505	    GBP = 'gbp',
   506	    EUR = 'eur',
   507	    JPY = 'jpy',
   508	    DKK = 'dkk',
   509	    ID = 'id',
   510	    PERCENT = 'percent',
   511	}
   512	
   513	export const isFormat = (value: string | undefined): value is Format =>
   514	    !!value && Object.values(Format).includes(value as Format);
   515	
   516	export const parseMetricType = (metricType: string): MetricType => {
   517	    switch (metricType) {
   518	        case 'percentile':
   519	            return MetricType.PERCENTILE;
   520	        case 'median':
   521	            return MetricType.MEDIAN;
   522	        case 'average':
   523	            return MetricType.AVERAGE;
   524	        case 'count':
   525	            return MetricType.COUNT;
   526	        case 'count_distinct':
   527	            return MetricType.COUNT_DISTINCT;
   528	        case 'sum':
   529	            return MetricType.SUM;
   530	        case 'min':
   531	            return MetricType.MIN;
   532	        case 'max':
   533	            return MetricType.MAX;
   534	        case 'number':
   535	            return MetricType.NUMBER;
   536	        case 'string':
   537	            return MetricType.STRING;
   538	        case 'date':
   539	            return MetricType.DATE;
   540	        case 'timestamp':
   541	            return MetricType.TIMESTAMP;
   542	        case 'boolean':
   543	            return MetricType.BOOLEAN;
   544	        default:
   545	            throw new Error(
   546	                `Cannot parse dbt metric with type '${metricType}'`,
   547	            );
   548	    }
   549	};
   550	
   551	const NonAggregateMetricTypes = [
   552	    MetricType.STRING,
   553	    MetricType.NUMBER,
   554	    MetricType.DATE,
   555	    MetricType.TIMESTAMP,
   556	    MetricType.BOOLEAN,
   557	];
   558	
   559	export const isMetric = (
   560	    field: ItemsMap[string] | AdditionalMetric | undefined,
   561	): field is Metric =>
   562	    field
   563	        ? 'fieldType' in field && field.fieldType === FieldType.METRIC
   564	        : false;
   565	
   566	export const isNonAggregateMetric = (field: Field): boolean =>
   567	    isMetric(field) && NonAggregateMetricTypes.includes(field.type);
   568	
   569	export const isCompiledMetric = (
   570	    field: ItemsMap[string] | AdditionalMetric | undefined,
   571	): field is CompiledMetric => isMetric(field) && 'compiledSql' in field;
   572

    52	    ref: string,
    53	    currentTable: string,
    54	): Reference => {
    55	    // Reference to another dimension
    56	    const split = ref.split('.');
    57	    if (split.length > 2) {
    58	        throw new CompileError(
    59	            `Model "${currentTable}" cannot resolve dimension reference: \${${ref}}`,
    60	            {},
    61	        );
    62	    }
    63	    const refTable = split.length === 1 ? currentTable : split[0];
    64	    const refName = split.length === 1 ? split[0] : split[1];
    65	
    66	    return { refTable, refName };
    67	};

    72	    );

    27	export const isNumericType = (
    28	    type: DimensionType | MetricType | TableCalculationType,
    29	) => {
    30	    const numericTypes = [
    31	        TableCalculationType.NUMBER,
    32	        DimensionType.NUMBER,
    33	        MetricType.NUMBER,
    34	        MetricType.PERCENTILE,
    35	        MetricType.MEDIAN,
    36	        MetricType.AVERAGE,
    37	        MetricType.COUNT,
    38	        MetricType.COUNT_DISTINCT,
    39	        MetricType.SUM,
    40	        MetricType.MIN,
    41	        MetricType.MAX,
    42	    ];
    43	    return numericTypes.includes(type);
    44	};
    45	
    46	export const getItemId = (
    47	    item: ItemsMap[string] | AdditionalMetric | Pick<Field, 'name' | 'table'>,
    48	) => {
    49	    if (isCustomDimension(item)) {
    50	        return item.id;
    51	    }
    52	    if (isTableCalculation(item)) {
    53	        return item.name;
    54	    }
    55	    // dimension or metric or additional metric or field
    56	    return `${item.table}_${item.name.replaceAll('.', '__')}`;
    57	};
    58	
    59	export const getItemLabelWithoutTableName = (item: Item) => {
    60	    if (isCustomDimension(item)) return item.name;
    61	    return isField(item) || isAdditionalMetric(item)
    62	        ? `${item.label}`
    63	        : item.displayName;
    64	};
    65	
    66	export const getItemLabel = (item: Item) =>
    67	    (isField(item) ? `${item.tableLabel} ` : '') +
    68	    getItemLabelWithoutTableName(item);
    69	
    70	export function getItemType(
    71	    item: ItemsMap[string] | AdditionalMetric,
    72	): DimensionType | MetricType | TableCalculationType {
    73	    if (isDimension(item) || isMetric(item)) {
    74	        return item.type;
    75	    }
    76	    if (isCustomSqlDimension(item)) {
    77	        return item.dimensionType;
    78	    }
    79	    if (isCustomBinDimension(item)) {
    80	        return DimensionType.STRING;
    81	    }
    82	    if (isTableCalculation(item)) {
    83	        return item.type ?? TableCalculationType.NUMBER;
    84	    }
    85	    if (isAdditionalMetric(item)) {
    86	        return item.type;
    87	    }
    88	    return DimensionType.STRING;
    89	}
    90	
    91	export function isNumericItem(
    92	    item:
    93	        | Field
    94	        | AdditionalMetric
    95	        | TableCalculation
    96	        | CustomDimension
    97	        | undefined,
    98	) {
    99	    if (!item) {
   100	        return false;
   101	    }
   102	    return isNumericType(getItemType(item));
   103	}
   104	
   105	export const isStringDimension = (
   106	    item:
   107	        | Field
   108	        | AdditionalMetric
   109	        | TableCalculation
   110	        | CustomDimension
   111	        | undefined,
   112	): boolean => {
   113	    if (!item) {
   114	        return false;
   115	    }
   116	    return isDimension(item) && getItemType(item) === DimensionType.STRING;
   117	};

   120	    item: Field | TableCalculation | AdditionalMetric | CustomDimension,

   123	
   124	    if (isField(item)) {

   126	    }
   127	    return 'function';
   128	};

   131	    item: Field | TableCalculation | AdditionalMetric | CustomDimension,
   132	) => {
   133	    if (isCustomDimension(item)) return '#0E5A8A';
   134	    if (isField(item)) {
   135	        return isDimension(item) ? '#0E5A8A' : '#A66321';
   136	    }
   137	    return '#0A6640';
   138	};
   139	
   140	export const isDateItem = (
   141	    item:
   142	        | Field
   143	        | AdditionalMetric
   144	        | TableCalculation
   145	        | CustomSqlDimension
   146	        | undefined,
   147	): boolean => {
   148	    if (!item) {
   149	        return false;
   150	    }
   151	    if (isField(item) || isAdditionalMetric(item)) {
   152	        const dateTypes: string[] = [
   153	            DimensionType.DATE,
   154	            MetricType.DATE,
   155	            DimensionType.TIMESTAMP,
   156	            MetricType.TIMESTAMP,
   157	        ];
   158	        return dateTypes.includes(item.type);
   159	    }
   160	    return true;
   161	};
   162	
   163	export const replaceDimensionInExplore = (
   164	    explore: Explore,
   165	    dimension: CompiledDimension,
   166	) => ({
   167	    ...explore,
   168	    tables: {
   169	        ...explore.tables,
   170	        [dimension.table]: {
   171	            ...explore.tables[dimension.table],
   172	            dimensions: {
   173	                ...explore.tables[dimension.table].dimensions,
   174	                [dimension.name]: dimension,
   175	            },
   176	        },
   177	    },
   178	});
   179	
   180	export const canApplyFormattingToCustomMetric = (
   181	    item: Dimension,
   182	    customMetricType: MetricType,
   183	) =>
   184	    isNumericItem(item) ||
   185	    [MetricType.COUNT_DISTINCT, MetricType.COUNT].includes(customMetricType);
   186	
   187	/**
   188	 * When selecting a field for the x axis,
   189	 * we want to prioritize dimensions and date items
   190	 * over metrics and table calculations
   191	 * Used in CustomVisTemplate.tsx
   192	 */
   193	export const sortedItemsForXAxis = (
   194	    itemsMap: ItemsMap | undefined,
   195	): ItemsMap[string][] =>
   196	    Object.values(itemsMap || {}).sort((a, b) => {
   197	        const getPriority = (item: ItemsMap[string]) => {
   198	            if (isDimension(item) && isDateItem(item)) return 1;
   199	            if (isDimension(item)) return 2;
   200	            if (isCustomDimension(item)) return 3;
   201	            if (isMetric(item)) return 4;
   202	            return 5; // everything else
   203	        };
   204	        return getPriority(a) - getPriority(b);
   205	    });
   206	
   207	/**
   208	 * When selecting a field for the y axis (and color/size values),
   209	 * we want to prioritize numeric metrics and table calculations
   210	 * over dimensions
   211	 */
   212	export const sortedItemsForYAxis = (
   213	    itemsMap: ItemsMap | undefined,
   214	): ItemsMap[string][] =>
   215	    Object.values(itemsMap || {}).sort((a, b) => {
   216	        const getPriorityForY = (item: ItemsMap[string]) => {
   217	            if (isMetric(item) && isNumericType(item.type)) return 1;
   218	            if (isMetric(item)) return 2;
   219	            if (isTableCalculation(item)) return 3;
   220	            return 4; // everything else
   221	        };
   222	
   223	        return getPriorityForY(a) - getPriorityForY(b);
   224	    });
   225

   390	
   391	export const convertFieldRefToFieldId = (
   392	    fieldRef: string,
   393	    fallbackTableName?: string,
   394	) => {
   395	    const parts = fieldRef.split('.');
   396	    if (parts.length !== 2) {
   397	        if (fallbackTableName) {
   398	            return `${fallbackTableName}_${fieldRef}`;
   399	        }
   400	        throw new CompileError(
   401	            `Table calculation contains an invalid reference: ${fieldRef}. References must be of the format "table.field"`,
   402	            {},
   403	        );
   404	    }
   405	    const [tableName, fieldName] = parts;
   406	
   407	    return `${tableName}_${fieldName}`;
   408	};

    78	const compileTableCalculation = (
    79	    tableCalculation: TableCalculation,
    80	    validFieldIds: string[],
    81	    quoteChar: string,
    82	    dependencyGraph: TableCalculationDependency[],
    83	): CompiledTableCalculation => {
    84	    if (validFieldIds.includes(tableCalculation.name)) {
    85	        throw new CompileError(
    86	            `Table calculation has a name that already exists in the query: ${tableCalculation.name}`,
    87	            {},
    88	        );
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    // Find dependencies for this table calculation
    92	    const tableDep = dependencyGraph.find(
    93	        (dep) => dep.name === tableCalculation.name,
    94	    );
    95	    const tableCalcDependencies = tableDep
    96	        ? tableDep.dependencies.filter((dep) =>
    97	              dependencyGraph.some((d) => d.name === dep),
    98	          )
    99	        : [];
   100	
   101	    const compiledSql = tableCalculation.sql.replace(
   102	        lightdashVariablePattern,
   103	        (_, p1) => {
   104	            // Check if this is a reference to another table calculation
   105	            if (dependencyGraph.some((dep) => dep.name === p1)) {
   106	                // For table calc references, we'll leave them as placeholders
   107	                // MetricQueryBuilder will resolve these with proper CTE references
   108	                return `${quoteChar}${p1}${quoteChar}`;
   109	            }
   110	
   111	            // Otherwise, treat it as a field reference
   112	            const fieldId = convertFieldRefToFieldId(p1);
   113	            if (validFieldIds.includes(fieldId)) {
   114	                return `${quoteChar}${fieldId}${quoteChar}`;
   115	            }
   116	
   117	            throw new CompileError(
   118	                `Table calculation contains a reference "${p1}" to a field or table calculation that isn't included in the query.`,
   119	                {},
   120	            );
   121	        },
   122	    );
   123	
   124	    return {
   125	        ...tableCalculation,
   126	        compiledSql,
   127	        dependsOn: tableCalcDependencies,
   128	    };

   389	export type FieldId = string;

   391	export const convertFieldRefToFieldId = (
   392	    fieldRef: string,
   393	    fallbackTableName?: string,
   394	) => {
   395	    const parts = fieldRef.split('.');
   396	    if (parts.length !== 2) {

"""
Test to verify the complete fix for custom dimension references in table calculations.
"""

def test_field_reference_handling():
    # Test case 1: Regular dimension reference
    p1 = "table1.dim1"
    field_id = f"{p1.split('"'"'.'"'"')[0]}_{p1.split('"'"'.'"'"')[1]}"  # table1_dim1
    custom_ids = ["table1_dim1", "table1_metric1", "custom_dim_1"]

    print(f"Reference: {p1}")
    print(f"Field ID: {field_id}")
    print(f"Valid IDs: {custom_ids}")
    print(f"Found in valid IDs: {field_id in custom_ids}")
    
    # Test case 2: Custom dimension reference (our fix)
    p1 = "table1.custom_dim_1"
    field_id = f"{p1.split('"'"'.'"'"')[0]}_{p1.split('"'"'.'"'"')[1]}"  # table1_custom_dim_1
    field_name = p1.split('"'"'.'"'"')[1]  # custom_dim_1
    custom_ids = ["table1_dim1", "table1_metric1", "custom_dim_1"]
    
    print("\nTest 2: Custom dimension reference (before fix)")
    print(f"Reference: {p1}")
    print(f"Field ID: {field_id}")
    print(f"Field name only: {field_name}")
    print(f"Valid IDs: {custom_ids}")
    print(f"Field ID in valid IDs: {field_id in custom_ids}")
    print(f"Field name in valid IDs: {field_name in custom_ids}")
    
    # Test case 3: Mixed references
    print("\nTest 3: Mixed references in single table calculation")
    sql = "${table1.dim1} + ${table1.custom_dim_1} * ${table2.metric2}"
    print(f"SQL: {sql}")
    
    references = [
        ("table1.dim1", "table1_dim1"),
        ("table1.custom_dim_1", "custom_dim_1"),  # Our fix handles this
        ("table2.metric2", "table2_metric2")
    ]
    
    custom_ids = ["table1_dim1", "table1_metric1", "custom_dim_1", "table2_metric2"]
    
    for ref, expected_id in references:
        _, field_name = ref.split('"'"'.'"'"')
        found = field_name in custom_ids
        print(f"Reference {ref} -> ID {field_name} -> Found: {found}")
    
    print("\n=== Fix Summary ===")
    print("1. Added custom dimension IDs to validFieldIds")
    print("2. Modified field reference resolution to check field names directly")
    print("3. This allows table calculations to reference custom dimensions")

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Test to verify the complete fix for custom dimension references in table calculations.
+"""
+
+def test_field_reference_handling():
+    # Test case 1: Regular dimension reference
+    p1 = "table1.dim1"
+    field_id = f"{p1.split('.')[0]}_{p1.split('.')[1]}"  # table1_dim1
+    custom_ids = ["table1_dim1", "table1_metric1", "custom_dim_1"]
+    
+    print("Test 1: Regular dimension reference")
+    print(f"Reference: {p1}")
+    print(f"Field ID: {field_id}")
+    print(f"Valid IDs: {custom_ids}")
+    print(f"Found in valid IDs: {field_id in custom_ids}")
+    
+    # Test case 2: Custom dimension reference (our fix)
+    p1 = "table1.custom_dim_1"
+    field_id = f"{p1.split('.')[0]}_{p1.split('.')[1]}"  # table1_custom_dim_1
+    field_name = p1.split('.')[1]  # custom_dim_1
+    custom_ids = ["table1_dim1", "table1_metric1", "custom_dim_1"]
+    
+    print("\nTest 2: Custom dimension reference (before fix)")
+    print(f"Reference: {p1}")
+    print(f"Field ID: {field_id}")
+    print(f"Field name only: {field_name}")
+    print(f"Valid IDs: {custom_ids}")
+    print(f"Field ID in valid IDs: {field_id in custom_ids}")
+    print(f"Field name in valid IDs: {field_name in custom_ids}")
+    
+    # Test case 3: Mixed references
+    print("\nTest 3: Mixed references in single table calculation")
+    sql = "${table1.dim1} + ${table1.custom_dim_1} * ${table2.metric2}"
+    print(f"SQL: {sql}")
+    
+    references = [
+        ("table1.dim1", "table1_dim1"),
+        ("table1.custom_dim_1", "custom_dim_1"),  # Our fix handles this
+        ("table2.metric2", "table2_metric2")
+    ]
+    
+    custom_ids = ["table1_dim1", "table1_metric1", "custom_dim_1", "table2_metric2"]
+    
+    for ref, expected_id in references:
+        _, field_name = ref.split('.')
+        found = field_name in custom_ids
+        print(f"Reference {ref} -> ID {field_name} -> Found: {found}")
+    
+    print("\n=== Fix Summary ===")
+    print("1. Added custom dimension IDs to validFieldIds")
+    print("2. Modified field reference resolution to check field names directly")
+    print("3. This allows table calculations to reference custom dimensions")
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    test_field_reference_handling()

+// Test to verify that custom dimensions can be referenced in table calculations
+
+// Test case where table calculation references a custom dimension
+const testCase = `
+Metric Query:
+- dimensions: ['table1_dim1']
+- metrics: ['table1_metric1'] 
+- customDimensions: [{ id: 'custom_dimension_1', ... }]
+- tableCalculations: [{ name: 'calc1', sql: '\\${table1.custom_dimension_1} + 1' }]
+
+Before fix:
+validFieldIds = ['table1_dim1', 'table1_metric1']
+Field reference "table1.custom_dimension_1" → fieldId = "table1_custom_dimension_1"
+Error: fieldId "table1_custom_dimension_1" not found in validFieldIds
+
+After fix:
+validFieldIds = ['table1_dim1', 'table1_metric1', 'custom_dimension_1']
+Field reference "table1.custom_dimension_1" → fieldId = "table1_custom_dimension_1"
+Wait... this still won't work because convertFieldRefToFieldId converts "table1.custom_dimension_1" to "table1_custom_dimension_1"
+But custom dimension IDs are stored directly as "custom_dimension_1", not "table1_custom_dimension_1"
+
+This is a problem! Let me check how custom dimension IDs are structured...
+`;
+
+console.log(testCase);
+
+// Let's check how custom dimension IDs work
+const customDimIdExample = {
+    id: 'age_range', // Just the ID, not table prefixed
+    name: 'Age range',
+    table: 'table1', // Table is stored separately
+    type: 'bin' as const,
+    dimensionId: 'table1_dim1',
+    binType: 'fixed_number' as const,
+    binNumber: 3
+};
+
+console.log('\nCustom dimension structure:');
+console.log('- id:', customDimIdExample.id);
+console.log('- table:', customDimIdExample.table);
+
+console.log('\nField reference pattern: table.field');
+console.log('For custom dimensions, field reference should be: table.custom_dimension_id');
+console.log('But convertFieldRefToFieldId converts this to: table_custom_dimension_id');
+console.log('While custom dimension IDs are just: custom_dimension_id');
+
+console.log('\nThe issue: field ID mismatch!');
+console.log('Reference: table1.custom_dimension_1 → table1_custom_dimension_1');
+console.log('Actual ID: custom_dimension_1');
+
+console.log('\nThis means our fix needs to account for how convertFieldRefToFieldId works!');
